# 灭却师

<body>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灭却师</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">血统</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><?xml:namespace 
prefix = "o" ns = "urn:schemas-microsoft-com:office:office" 
/><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">本质：特异本质</font> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">原典：死神《</font><font face="宋体">bleach》</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">作者：苍蓝宿命三号机</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">所有灭却师均有祖先友哈巴赫的血统，拥有从外界环境中摄取灵子的能力，经过强化后此能力可以把由灵子构成的物质分解吸收，或阻止死神利用空气中灵子形成立足点。极少数的灭却师族人无法吸收灵子，这种灭却师拥有与其祖先友哈巴赫一样拥有与</font><font face="宋体">“摄取灵子”相反的“赋予灵魂”的能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注：圣文字因为种类繁多，本文本主要列举了灭却师一脉的通用技能，圣文字相关的技能请详情参照文本</font><font face="宋体">-圣文字篇。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注：本血统是人类血统</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">能量池：灵力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启灭却师</font><font face="宋体">D级技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">和专属物品购买权</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特性：灵子强化</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">、</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灭却灵箭</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵子强化：你手持的武器获得【心灵武器】特性，若已经拥有该特性，则改为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你的心灵检定</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">获得</font><font face="宋体">1点附加成功。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灭却灵箭：你以心灵检定进行远程攻击时，该攻击获得</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">点【破魔】，若已具备等额或者更高的【破魔】，则改为增加</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">点【破魔】。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">C级</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">价格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">C+1200</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">属性：决心</font><font face="宋体">+2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">沉着</font><font face="宋体">+2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启灭却师</font><font face="宋体">C级技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特性：动血装</font><font face="宋体">/静血装（双特性）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">动血装</font><font face="宋体">/静血装</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">是</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">纯血种灭却师与生俱来的能力，直接将灵子注入到血管中，将肉体的防御力极大地提升，但使用静血装时不能使用动血装。动血装直接将灵子注入到血管中，将发挥出的破坏力极大地提升，但使用动血装时不能使用静血装。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">动血装</font><font face="宋体">/静血装：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你可以以自由动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/反射动作在动血装和静血装中切换，两个血装不能同时存在，分别具备不同的能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">选择动血装：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你获得一个增幅能力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">-</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你进行心灵检定时，可以无需动作额外积累灵感疲劳进行增幅，你每有</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1点传奇决心，就可以额外积累3点灵感疲劳增幅一次，每次增幅使你此次心灵检定获得6DP能量加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">被认为是有哈巴赫赐予坐下灭却师的能力，也有一种说法是认为灭却师灵魂的本质力量被有哈巴赫的血所引发的觉醒，不管哪种说法，都是极大程度解放了其自身所隐藏的能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">圣文字：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你的灵力池上限增加你的（决心值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">+沉着值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你以心灵检定进行的远程攻击</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">，有一半的伤害会提升为恶性伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">若你购买本级血统时尚未开启三阶本能觉醒，则你现在开启三阶本能觉醒，但是你的四阶本能觉醒的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">DC会因此增加3点（即由原本的4D10出目36开启4阶本能觉醒变为4D10出目39才能开启4阶本能觉醒）；若你</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">购买本级血统时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">已经开启三阶本能觉醒，则你以心灵检定进行远程攻击时，你的攻击检定获得你沉着值</font><font face="宋体">*1DP内在加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">此外，你本能觉醒中的</font><font face="宋体">“智力”关键字被“决心”替代（例如一阶本能觉醒的效果“你在使用意志力的基础用法时，可以获得等于感知和智力中较低者的完美加值。”现在变为“你在使用意志力的基础用法时，可以获得等于感知和决心中较低者的完美加值。”）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特殊：购买</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S级血统前，PC需要进行一次判定-若PC购买本级血统前同时已经购买了B级以上支线等级的死神称号和虚化改造，则强化本级血统时可以选择分支-灵王后补。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S级</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的子嗣（有哈巴赫）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">价格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S+14400</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">属性：决心</font><font face="宋体">+16，沉着+16</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启灭却师</font><font face="宋体">S级技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">和</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S级圣文字技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特性：灵王之子（双特性）灭却师之王</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">被认为灵王之子的有哈巴赫，自然拥有着跟灵王同等的神力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">在昆西的传说中，有一首歌叫做《圣帝颂歌》（カイザー</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 微软雅黑; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="微软雅黑">?</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">ゲザング，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Kaizā 
Gezangu；德语为“皇帝之歌”，日语为“神圣皇帝的赞歌”；即 “国王的赞美诗”）讲述了一位被封印的灭却师之王。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">根据歌中的说法，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">被封印的灭却师之王，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">经过</font><font face="宋体">900年取回心跳，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">再经过</font><font face="宋体">90年取回意识，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">再经过</font><font face="宋体">9年取回力量。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">为了恢复自身力量，灭却师之王必须取回</font><font face="宋体">“不纯洁”的灭却师的力量。当友哈巴赫窃取了黑崎真咲和片桐叶绘的力量时，这个传说被证实了。然而，根据友哈巴赫的说法，这首歌还有额外的部分：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">当他重新获得力量</font><font face="宋体">9天后，皇帝将重新夺回这个世界。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王之子：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你获得超凡神圣，获得</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">0级神格。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">当你施展以心灵检定发动的能力时，若该能力是造成伤害，则无论其原本是否可以豁免，则现在均变为不可豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灭却师之王</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">：每场冒险世界一次，当你死亡后，你会在死亡的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">9秒后（即下一轮结束时）/9轮后/9小时后/9天后/9个月后/9年后/</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">90年</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">后</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/900年后原地复活，具体复活时机由你选择。你复活时，你的生命值全部恢复至满值，你的全部通用能量池和特殊能量池均恢复至满值，你的意志力池恢复至满值，你死亡时承受的所有状态和BUFF被全部移除（不分正负面），并且移除死亡时承受的全部不良状态点数，你的所有刻度则保持在死亡时的状态。若你是选择死亡后的9秒后复活，则你复活时，你会获得完整的一个回合，在你执行完这个回合后，战斗轮才会按照顺序开启新的一轮。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注意：若你选择的复活时间过长，导致你复活前你的队友就完成了任务返回轮回之境，这会导致你被滞留于冒险世界无法返回（通常情况下，这被判定为玩家的角色并未死亡，但是玩家的跑团至此结束）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S级</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王候补</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">价格：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">S+14400</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">强化</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">前提：购买</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">本级</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">血统时同时兼有</font><font face="宋体">B级以上的死神称号与虚化改造</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">属性：决心</font><font face="宋体">+16，沉着+16</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">技能树：开启灭却师</font><font face="宋体">S级技能树</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特性：灵王候补（双特性）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你现在同时拥有了三界的力量，可以作为世界的稳定</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Segoe UI Symbol'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Segoe UI Symbol'; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Segoe UI Symbol'"><font face="宋体">之锚，亦可以凭借自身的能力创造新的未来。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">作为虚，完现术，死神，灭却师力量的来源，其本身视为世界所有的起源之力。</font> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王候补：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你获得超凡神圣，获得</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">0级神格。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">当你施展以心灵检定发动的能力时，若该能力是造成伤害，则无论其原本是否可以豁免，则现在均变为不可豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流：灵王的奔流：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你获得一个新的能量池</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">-灵王的奔流。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">本质：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特异</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">这是一个特殊能量池。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">是一种精神力量，拥有这种力量的人可以行走于生国与死境之间，模糊了魂与物的界限。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">是精神的体现，因此使用</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">并不一定需要</font><font face="宋体">“付出”特定的能量。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流的大小：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你获得</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">能量池时，你会失去你全部的关键属性包含心智系属性的通用能量池并且也不能再获得这些能量池，然后结算这些通用能量池的当前上限，你的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">能量池的上限等同这些能量池的上限之和。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注意：若你的这些通用能量池原本拥有提升了上限的效果，则按照上限提升之后的能量池数值进行结算，但是只结算永久持续的上限，任何临时提升能量池上限的能力不计入其中（例如你的精神力能量池通过通脉丹提升了</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">10点能量池上限，同时你拥有一个技能，可以使你在一个场景内临时获得20点精神力能量池上限，则通脉丹提升的永久性10点精神力能量池上限能够生效，而你的技能提升的临时的20点精神力能量池上限无法生效</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注意：你获得</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">能量池后，你因此失去的那些通用能量池在判定上变为不存在，所有会影响这些通用能量池的能力（无论正负面），均无法再影响你。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">注意：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流自身无法获得任何提升能量池上限的能力，灵王的奔流池自身的上限与其所有合并的能量池相关。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流的基础用法：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1、灵王的奔流可以按照其所合并的所有能量池使用其基础用法，并且若带来的加值相同，改为可以叠加。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">如：灵王的奔流吞噬了灵力与精神力，则可以分别使用它们的基础用法，但是你的灵王的奔流没有合并魔力，则无法使用魔力的基础用法。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2、战斗中，你可以每回合开始时无需动作支付1点灵王的奔流，使自身获得相当于基础移动速度的飞行能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">非战斗中，你可以每</font><font face="宋体">10分钟支付1点灵王的奔流，使自身获得相当于基础移动速度三倍的旅行速度。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3、你可以支付5点灵王的奔流，使自身免疫环境带来的负面影响，如极限温度，宇宙，真空，高压等。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">4、当你进行任何属性检定时，你无需动作可以花费1点灵王的奔流，使该检定获得3DP完美加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流的特殊性：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1、灵王的奔流在判定上既不属于心智系能量池也属于心智系能量池</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">这取决于如何对使用者有利。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">（也就是说，巨龙无法免疫灵王的奔流造成的效果，但是若你获得心智系能量池加强的效果，在灵王的奔流的作用下，其可以如常生效）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2、当使用者需要消耗心智</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">系通用</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">能量池</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">的能力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">时，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">若该心智系通用能量池已被</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">合并，则</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流可以无条件代替该能量池使用。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3、若一个能量池无法兼容其他能量池，当被灵王的奔流吞噬后，失去该限制。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">4、灵王的奔流本身是特殊能量池，所以其既非东方能量池，也非西方能量池。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">5、你因为使用灵力技能而累积灵力疲劳时，改为消耗等量的灵王的奔流。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 等线; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">灵王的奔流的恢复：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">效果：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你进行一次心灵检定，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">移除你此次心灵检定成功数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/2点灵感疲劳。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">本技能每</font><font face="宋体">2次长休间最多使用一次。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">特殊：本技能会导致</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">范围内所有的灵子不再有剩余，除非经过</font><font face="宋体">1个月或者更换场地又或者更长的时间，才能重新从这片区域获取灵子</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">-这意味着有单位使用此技能后，其他单位在该范围内使用此技能时也无法以此技能移除灵感疲劳；此外，该范围内因为灵力归零，因此除你之外的所有单位将无法使用灵力相关的增幅能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">研发：当你的血统到达</font><font face="宋体">B级时，你可以消耗54XP进行研发</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">，研发完成后本技能更名为</font><font face="宋体">“</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">圣隶</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">”，启动</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">DC提升为15，范围变为半径5000米，效果变更为-</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你进行一次心灵检定，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">移除你此次心灵检定成功数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/点灵感疲劳。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">效果：你</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">进行一次心灵检定，此次心灵检定你获得你决心值</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">*1DP招式加值和你传奇决心*2点附加成功，对范围内造成检定成功数/点神圣严重伤害，受影响的目标以反射豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">若有单位因为本技能而受到伤害，则其攻击检定或者三豁免检定或者防御会承受豁免差值</font><font face="宋体">/点招式减值（由你在施展本技能时决定），持续至你停止引导为止。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">持续：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：圣隶的高位使用方式，雨龙的战斗术，可以通过聚集周围的灵子产生如万羽般的箭矢，以无法反应的高速生成绝对隶属的五芒星单体阵法，剥夺敌人灵力的同时封锁敌人的卍解。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">效果：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你以心灵检定对目标进行一次远程心灵攻击，你的心灵检定获得你传奇决心</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">*2点附加成功，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">对目标造成神圣严重伤害，并且你选择目标所拥有的一个关键属性包含心智属性的通用能量池，使该能量池流失你此次攻击检定成功数</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">/点能量，若目标没有任何可供流失能量的</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">关键属性包含心智属性的通用能量池（或者当前的能量池中的剩余能量低于你此次攻击检定成功数），则改为流失等额的意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">若本技能成功对目标造成伤害，则目标以你此次心灵检定成功数为</font><font face="宋体">DC进行一次意志豁免，若其豁免失败，则你选择你曾亲眼目睹过目标施展的一项A级以下支线级别的能力，将该能力封印豁免差值/轮，这是一个封印效果。若目标有能力因此而被你封印，则你施展本技能时的全部基础能耗会返还给你。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">从下一轮开始，目标每回合结束时，可以以</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">你此次心灵检定成功数为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">DC进行一次意志豁免，若豁免成功，则摆脱该封印状态；若豁免失败，则目标下一次对此进行反射豁免检定时获得6DP完美加值，无限叠加，直至摆脱该封印状态。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">增幅：你每有</font><font face="宋体">1点传奇沉着，则施展本技能时额外积累7点灵感疲劳进行增幅，每次增幅使你此次心灵检定获得你决心值*1DP招式加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">描述：他们花费了</font><font face="宋体">1000年的时间，躲在影子内操纵灵子、构筑灵子空间，因此自称“无形帝国”，同时为以后的战斗蓄积力量。战后900年，友哈巴赫恢复了心跳，又过90年，友哈巴赫恢复了意识。就在黑崎一护9岁那年，友哈巴赫用“圣别”强行将全世界所有混血灭却师的灵力取走，以恢复往日的力量。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
